prepared.module target=riscv64-linux-gnu route=semantic_bir_shared
completed_phases: legalize stack_layout liveness out_of_ssa regalloc
invariants:
  - no_target_facing_i1
  - no_phi_nodes
notes:
  - [prealloc] prealloc owns the shared semantic-BIR to prealloc-BIR route before MIR lowering
  - [legalize] bootstrap BIR legalize kept semantic CFG and phi form intact while promoting i1 values plus function signature/storage bookkeeping, memory-address/load-store bookkeeping, and call ABI metadata
  - [stack_layout] stack layout prepared function 'swap' with 1 home slot(s) and 4 bytes of frame space
  - [stack_layout] stack layout prepared function 'partition' with 4 home slot(s) and 16 bytes of frame space
  - [stack_layout] stack layout prepared function 'quicksort' with 1 home slot(s) and 4 bytes of frame space
  - [stack_layout] stack layout prepared function 'main' with 1 home slot(s) and 4 bytes of frame space
  - [stack_layout] stack layout now emits provisional stack objects, elides dead and copy-coalesced home slots, and only allocates frame storage for objects that still require dedicated homes
  - [liveness] liveness now computes BIR named-value intervals, exact def/use program points, predecessor-edge phi uses, call points, CFG-aware live-through extension, and loop depth independently of stack-layout object identity
  - [out_of_ssa] out_of_ssa removed phi nodes from live prepared BIR and published authoritative join-transfer plus parallel-copy obligations
  - [regalloc] regalloc seeded function 'swap' with 133 allocation constraint(s) and 899 interference edge(s) from active liveness; assigned 38 register(s) and 95 stack slot(s)
  - [regalloc] regalloc seeded function 'partition' with 81 allocation constraint(s) and 695 interference edge(s) from active liveness; assigned 19 register(s) and 62 stack slot(s)
  - [regalloc] regalloc seeded function 'quicksort' with 8 allocation constraint(s) and 15 interference edge(s) from active liveness; assigned 6 register(s) and 2 stack slot(s)
  - [regalloc] regalloc seeded function 'main' with 80 allocation constraint(s) and 736 interference edge(s) from active liveness; assigned 12 register(s) and 68 stack slot(s)

bir.func @quicksort(i32 %p.left, i32 %p.right) -> void {
entry:
  %t0 = bir.sge i32 %p.left, %p.right
  bir.cond_br i32 %t0, block_7, block_8
block_7:
  bir.ret
block_8:
  %t3 = bir.call i32 partition(i32 %p.left, i32 %p.right)
  ; call_arg_source index=0 encoding=register source_value_id=214 source_value=%p.left
  ; call_arg_source index=1 encoding=register source_value_id=215 source_value=%p.right
  bir.store_local %lv.index, i32 %t3
  %t4 = bir.load_local i32 %lv.index
  %t5 = bir.sub i32 %t4, 1
  bir.call void quicksort(i32 %p.left, i32 %t5)
  ; call_arg_source index=0 encoding=register source_value=%p.left
  ; call_arg_source index=1 encoding=register source_value=%t5
  %t6 = bir.load_local i32 %lv.index
  %t7 = bir.add i32 %t6, 1
  bir.call void quicksort(i32 %t7, i32 %p.right)
  ; call_arg_source index=0 encoding=register source_value=%t7
  ; call_arg_source index=1 encoding=register source_value=%p.right
  bir.ret
}

--- prepared-control-flow ---
prepared.func @swap
  block entry terminator=return
prepared.func @partition
  block entry terminator=branch target=for.cond.2
  block for.cond.2 terminator=cond_branch true=block_2 false=block_3
  block for.latch.2 terminator=branch target=for.cond.2
  block block_2 terminator=cond_branch true=block_4 false=block_5
  block block_3 terminator=return
  block block_4 terminator=branch target=block_5
  block block_5 terminator=branch target=for.latch.2
  branch_condition for.cond.2 kind=fused_compare condition=%t6 compare=slt i32 %t5, %p.right can_fuse_with_branch=yes true=block_2 false=block_3
  branch_condition block_2 kind=fused_compare condition=%t16 compare=slt i32 %t14.outer0, %t15 can_fuse_with_branch=yes true=block_4 false=block_5
prepared.func @quicksort
  block entry terminator=cond_branch true=block_7 false=block_8
  block block_7 terminator=return
  block block_8 terminator=return
  branch_condition entry kind=fused_compare condition=%t0 compare=sge i32 %p.left, %p.right can_fuse_with_branch=yes true=block_7 false=block_8

  block block_12 terminator=branch target=for.latch.12
  block block_13 terminator=return
  branch_condition for.cond.10 kind=fused_compare condition=%t33 compare=slt i32 %t32, 16 can_fuse_with_branch=yes true=block_10 false=block_11
  branch_condition for.cond.12 kind=fused_compare condition=%t47 compare=slt i32 %t46, 16 can_fuse_with_branch=yes true=block_12 false=block_13

--- prepared-storage-plans ---
